window.cookiePreference = function () {
  var gdprCookie =_satellite.cookie.get("cookieConfiguration")
  if(gdprCookie){
  	var Dcookie = JSON.parse(atob(gdprCookie));

    if (Dcookie.experienceAndInsight && !Dcookie.Marketing) {
      return "experience";
    } else if (!Dcookie.experienceAndInsight && !Dcookie.Marketing) {
      return "none";
    } else if (!Dcookie.experienceAndInsight && Dcookie.Marketing) {
      return "marketing";
    } else {
      return "all";
    }
  }else{
    return 'all';
  }
};
